
on_actions = {
	on_create_faction = {
		effect = {
			if = {				#from Polish decision where Lithuania reconciled the Wilno issue
				limit = { 
					original_tag = POL
					is_faction_leader = yes
					has_capitulated = no

					LIT = {
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction = no
						has_capitulated = no
						exists = yes
						has_country_flag = LIT_resolved_crisis
					}
				}
				POL = {
					country_event = { id = poland.133 days = 2 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				if = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GRE
						owns_state = 797
						controls_state = 797
						797 = { is_capital = yes }
						is_ai = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = democratic
						}
						set_faction_name = "Treaty of Constantinople"
						#news_event = { id = news.159 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = neutrality
						}
						set_faction_name = "Blachernae Protocols"
						#news_event = { id = news.159 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = fascism
						}
						set_faction_name = "Sacred Roman Treaty"
						#news_event = { id = news.159 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = GER
						is_ai = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = fascism
						}
						set_faction_name = "New Order"
						#news_event = { id = news.159 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ENG
						is_ai = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_government = democratic
						}
						set_faction_name = "Allied Nations"
						#news_event = { id = news.159 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = MEX
						has_government = neutrality
						is_ai = yes
					}
					set_faction_name = "Convention of Mexico"
					#news_event = { id = news.159 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = USA
						has_government = democratic
					}
					set_faction_name = "United Nations"
					#news_event = { id = news.159 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#ROOT is winner #FROM gets annexed - For civil wars on_civil_war_end is also fired
	on_annex = {
		effect = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						tag = DEN
					}
					den_become_generic = yes
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						tag = RAJ
					}
					load_focus_tree = r56_india_generic
					remove_ideas = {			
						RAJ_Agrarian_Economy
						RAJ_agrarian_economy_famine 
						RAJ_agrarian_economy_recovery 
						RAJ_agrarian_economy_1 
						RAJ_agrarian_economy_2 
					}
					clr_country_flag = election_enabled
					clr_country_flag = raj_election_over
					clr_country_flag = army_research_decision
					clr_country_flag = RAJ_rail_act_support
					clr_country_flag = RAJ_agri_act_support
					clr_country_flag = RAJ_war_act_support
					clr_country_flag = ilp_conference_concluded
					clr_country_flag = independence_granted 
					clr_country_flag = ilp_south_asian_liberation
					clr_country_flag = integration_of_india
					clr_country_flag = ILP_victory 
					clr_country_flag = UP_victory
					clr_country_flag = INC_victory
					remove_ideas_with_trait = militiant_independence_activist
					set_country_flag = RAJ_famine_manual_trigger 	#Prevents Famine, which is hard to deal with without the focus tree
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = neutrality
						name = "AIFB"
						long_name = "All India Forward Bloc"
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Subhas Chandra Bose"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/RAJ/r56_portrait_RAJ_Subhas_Chadra_Bose.dds"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = {
							indomitable_perseverance
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						tag = ENG
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							RAJ = {
								has_cosmetic_tag = RAJ_UK
							}
						}
						drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
						retire_character = RAJ_lord_linlithgow
						retire_character = RAJ_lord_willingdon
						retire_character = RAJ_archibald_wavell
						retire_character = RAJ_louis_mountbatten
						set_party_name = {
							ideology = neutrality
							name = "UP"
							long_name = "Unionist Party"
						}
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = CAN
					FROM = { tag = QBC }
				}
				#Quebec conscription crisis: Canada
				every_controlled_state = {				#start only in controlled states
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 466
							state = 468
							state = 860
							state = 861
							state = 862
							state = 863
						}
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = quebec_conscription_crisis
					}
					set_state_flag = quebec_conscription_crisis_flag
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = GER
					NOT = { has_government = democratic }
					date < 1941.01.01
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { tag = HOL } }
					USA = {
						set_country_flag = { flag = USA_dutch_window days = 60 value = 1 }
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
					USA = {
						set_country_flag = { flag = USA_british_window days = 120 value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { tag = CZE }
				}
				CZE = {
					set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = democratic
						popularity = 0.5
					}
					#load_focus_tree = generic_focus
					set_country_flag = hide_interwar_diplomacy
					mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
					remove_ideas = {
						emil_hacha
						CZKE_national_unity_government_idea
						CZKE_fifth_column
						CZKE_fifth_column_2
						CZKE_unruly_minorities
						CZKE_unruly_minorities_2
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							ENG = {
								has_government = democratic
								democratic > 0.35
							}
							ROOT = {
								NOT = { tag = ENG }
							}
						}
						every_operative = {
							limit = {
								has_trait = operative_double_agent
							}
							turn_operative = { turned_by = ENG }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			#probably remove in the future to avoid clones
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { tag = AUS }
					FROM = {
						tag = HUN
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				AUS = {
					create_operative_leader = {
						name = "Eugenio Zilahy Kiss"
						portrait_path = gfx/leaders/Europe/portrait_europe_generic_operative_male_5.dds
						traits = { operative_well_groomed }
						bypass_recruitment = no
						available_to_spy_master = yes
						nationalities = { HUN AUS ARG }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_independent_warlords = no
						NOT = { has_country_flag = is_warlords }
					}
					FROM = {
						tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { original_tag = FROM }
					}
					clear_global_event_target = KMT_central_gov_tag
				}
				else = {
					save_global_event_target_as = KMT_central_gov_tag
				}
			}
		}
	}

###---> On Capitulation <><> <><> <><>
	on_capitulation = { #ROOT is surrendering country, FROM is winner.
		effect = {
			if = {	#add unique conscription law upon capitulation- Fantom
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					any_other_country = {	#making sure they have some allies to host them
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
						has_war_with = FROM
					}
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							original_tag = CAN
							NOT = {
								has_completed_focus = r56_CAN_conscription_crisis
							}
						}
					}
					NOT = {	#no special things for anarchists
						AND = {
							original_tag = HON
							has_completed_focus = HON_free_our_markets
							has_idea = r56_idea_capitalism_anarchist_society
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							original_tag = SPR
							has_dlc = "La Resistance"
							has_completed_focus = SPR_all_must_bear_the_torch
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							original_tag = MON
							has_completed_focus = MON_changes_within
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = influx_of_exiles_r56_law	#conscription law
			}
			if = {	#add unique trade law upon capitulation
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					any_other_country = {	#making sure they have some allies to host them
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
						has_war_with = FROM
					}
					NOT = {	#no special things for anarchists
						AND = {
							original_tag = HON
							has_completed_focus = HON_free_our_markets
							has_idea = r56_idea_capitalism_anarchist_society
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							original_tag = SPR
							has_dlc = "La Resistance"
							has_completed_focus = SPR_all_must_bear_the_torch
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							original_tag = MON
							has_completed_focus = MON_changes_within
						}
					}
				}
				add_ideas = full_host_reliance_r56_law	#trade law
			}
			if = {	#add unique economy law upon capitulation
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					any_other_country = {	#making sure they have some allies to host them
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
						has_war_with = FROM
					}
					NOT = {	#no extra fun for anarchists
						has_idea = SPR_collectivized_society
					}
				}
				add_ideas = evacuated_assets_r56_law	#economy law
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_major = yes
				}
				set_major = no
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = ENG
					has_war_with = SCO
					SCO = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = SCO_has_the_stone_of_scone
						}
					}
				}
				SCO = {
					set_country_flag = SCO_has_the_stone_of_scone
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = SCO_absence_of_the_stone_of_scone
						}
						remove_ideas = SCO_absence_of_the_stone_of_scone
					}
				}
			}

			# Polish government goes into exile after the capitulation by both USSR and Germany
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = POL
					is_in_faction = yes							#have to be in faction
					has_war_with = GER
					has_war_with = SOV
					has_global_flag = sov_yes_pact
					has_idea = POL_shock_from_surprised_attack_idea	#only in this case the exile will work in such way
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = POL
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					POL = {
						become_exiled_in = {
							target = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = event_target:den_scw_volunteers_received
					original_tag = SPR
				}
				DEN = {
					add_manpower = 400 #TODO EVENT
				}

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = DEN
					NOT = { has_global_flag = DEN_use_DLC_tree }
					is_in_faction = yes	#don't fire the event if Denmark was alone and will be handled in the peace deal in a second - Illya
					FROM = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = democratic
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					DEN = {
						set_variable = {
							occupation_target = PREV
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						id = denmark.101
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = DEN
					OR = {
						ICE = { is_subject_of = DEN }
						DEN = { owns_state = 100 }
						ICE = { owns_state = 100 }
					}
					NOR = {
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = NOR_reclaim_the_islands
							has_completed_focus = NOR_icelandic-faroese_revolt
							has_completed_focus = NOR_reclaim_danish
							has_completed_focus = NOR_unite_the_scandinavian_workers
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = wtt_denmark.1 days = 1 }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = r56_aluminium_collection }
				add_resource = {
					type = aluminium
					amount = -1
				}
				clr_state_flag = r56_aluminium_collection
			}
			if = {	#moved from Belgian events	-	event about king Leopold Surrender
				limit = {
					original_tag = BEL
					has_idea = BEL_leopold3
					OR = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = belgium.62 hours = 12 }

			}
			if = { #
				limit = { tag = VIC }
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = free_france
					}
					annex_country = { target = VIC transfer_troops = yes }
				}
			}
			if = { #MOD. Small OPT
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					has_government = democratic
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = RAJ
						is_subject_of = ENG
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = MAL
						is_subject_of = ENG
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = INS
						is_subject_of = HOL
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = DNZ
					DNZ = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = r56_dnz_dont_lose_cores }
					}
					is_ai = yes
				}
				85 = { remove_core_of = DNZ }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = RUT
					RUT = {
						has_country_flag = r56_UPA_check
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						HUN = {
							exists = yes
						}
					}
					HUN = {
						country_event = { id = axis_minors_ruthenia.8 days = 1 }
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = RUT
						NOT = {
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = UKR
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = DOU
						}
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = r56_upa_state_modifier }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = CHI
					CHI = {
						has_completed_focus = KMT_the_big_rear_concept
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = r56_the_big_rear
						}
					}
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = r56_the_big_rear }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = r56_the_big_rear
						}
					}
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = r56_the_rear }
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = CHI
					CHI = {
						has_completed_focus = KMT_lure_them_in_strategy
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = r56_lure_them_in
						}
					}
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = r56_lure_them_in }
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = DEN
					OR = {
						ICE = { is_subject_of = DEN }
						DEN = { owns_state = 100 }
						ICE = { owns_state = 100 }
					}
					NOR = {
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = NOR_reclaim_the_islands
							has_completed_focus = NOR_icelandic-faroese_revolt
							has_completed_focus = NOR_reclaim_danish
							has_completed_focus = NOR_unite_the_scandinavian_workers
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = wtt_denmark.1 days = 1 }
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = SHX
							tag = GXC
							tag = XSM
							tag = YUN
							tag = SIK
							tag = TNG
							tag = CHI
						}
						has_country_flag = is_warlords
						is_in_faction_with = PRC
						has_idea = KMT_united_front
						has_completed_focus = CHI_cooperation_with_the_communists
					}
				}
				PRC = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.300 }
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = SHX
							tag = GXC
							tag = XSM
							tag = YUN
							tag = SIK
							tag = TNG
							tag = CHI
						}
						has_country_flag = is_warlords
						is_in_faction_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
						has_idea = KMT_united_front
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = CHI_cooperation_with_the_communists
						}
					}
				}
				event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.300 }
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						tag = MAN
						is_subject_of = JAP
						has_country_leader = {
							character = MAN_puyi
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						OR = {
							tag = CHI
							tag = PRC
							tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.303 }
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = PGR
							has_cosmetic_tag = HCPC
						}
						is_puppet_of = CHI
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					country_event = { id = kmt.300 }
				}
				MEN = {
					transfer_state = 611
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ITA
					ITA = {
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = ITA_royal_intervention
						}
						has_government = fascism
						has_completed_focus = ITA_militarize_the_rome_protocols
						has_war_with = GER
					}
					GER = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_war_with = ITA
					}
				}
				ITA = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = ITA_RSI
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = fascism
						long_name = "Partito Fascista Repubblicano"
						name = "PFR"
					}
					retire_ideology_leader = fascism
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = r56_ita_badoglio_is_leader
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_unit_leader = 690 }
							remove_unit_leader = 690
						}
						create_country_leader = {
							name = "Pietro Badoglio"
							picture = "gfx/leaders/ITA/Portrait_Italy_Pietro_Badoglio.dds"
							expire = "1965.1.1"
							ideology = fascism_ideology
							traits = {
								army_connections
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = POL }
				if = {
					limit = { has_unit_leader = 3180 }
					remove_unit_leader = 3180
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = POL_Draw_Closer_To_The_USSR }
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = POL_Seek_Autonomy }
					}
					POL = { set_party_name = { ideology = communism long_name = POL_GL_party_long name = POL_GL_party } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						POL = { is_puppet = no }
					}
					POL = { set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = POL_KN_party_long name = POL_KN_party } }
					POL = { set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = POL_ZWZ_party_long name = POL_ZWZ_party } }
					set_cosmetic_tag = POLAK
				}
				if = { #MOD. Optimized a little.
					limit = {
						POL = {
							has_civil_war = no
							is_puppet = no
							is_in_faction = yes
							NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_Exile_Government_Formed }
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = POL_Exile_Government_Formed
					if = {
						limit = { POL = { has_government = neutrality } }
						POL = { country_event = poland.196 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { POL = { has_government = democratic } }
						if = {
							limit = {
								POL = {
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = POL_The_Polish_Socialist_Party }
									NOT = { has_completed_focus = POL_The_Endecja_Movement }
								}
							}
							add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 1 }
							create_country_leader = {

	on_peaceconference_started = {
		effect = {

								has_war_with = JAP

							}
							any_owned_state = {
								is_core_of = FRI
							}

								exists = no
							}
						}

							limit = {
								is_core_of = FRI
							}
							set_state_flag = r56_postwar_transfer_to_fri

	on_civil_war_end_before_annexation = {

	on_subject_free = {
		effect = {
			if = { #retire colonial leader if gained independence
				limit = {
					tag = INS
					has_country_leader_ideology = colonial_government
				}
				retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
				country_event = { id = indonesia.107 hours = 12 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SAR
					has_cosmetic_tag = SAR_FRA
				}
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = yes
					NOT = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					has_war = no
					faction_leader = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}			
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = GAB
					has_cosmetic_tag = GAB_FRA
				}
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = MLI
					has_cosmetic_tag = MLI_FRA
				}
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}

						has_cosmetic_tag = MOR_SPR
						has_cosmetic_tag = MOR_FRA
					}

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SEN

				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes

			if = {

				if = {
					limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = SAF_ENG }
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
				if = {

###---> On Civil War End <><> <><> <><>
	#ROOT is winner #FROM gets annexed - This will also fire on_annex
	on_civil_war_end = {
		effect = {
			if = {# The Norwegian Monarchist Civil War has ended. Norway gets to choose how to deal with the opposition leaders
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						original_tag = NOR
						has_completed_focus = NOR_traditions_worth_fighting_for
						has_government = neutrality
						has_country_flag = NOR_has_monarchist_civil_war
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = naw_norway.141 days = 14 random_days = 2	}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						original_tag = INS
						has_completed_focus = INS_limited_autonomy
						has_war_with = HOL
					}
				}
				white_peace = HOL
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						original_tag = AFG
						has_government = fascism
						has_completed_focus = AFG_waaidu
					}
				}
				add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = -1 }
			}
			#Afghanistan Civil War Loss - skill issue you are monarchist now
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						original_tag = AFG
						NOT = {
							has_government = fascism
							has_idea = AFG_lawless_emirate
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						load_focus_tree = { tree = afghanistan_focus keep_completed = yes }
						mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
						uncomplete_national_focus = {
							focus = AFG_handle_the_king
							uncomplete_children = yes
							refund_political_power = no
						}
						unlock_national_focus = AFG_first_loya_jirga
						unlock_national_focus = AFG_power_to_the_king
						change_tag_from = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					TAG = EGY
					PAL = {
						has_country_flag = PAL_palestinian_aided_uprising
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = palestine.45
					days = 1
					random_hours = 12
				}
			}
			#Cordeanu's revolt
			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = ROM }
				#Cordeanu's revolt, iron guard victory
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_global_flag = cordeanu_civil_war
					}
					clr_global_flag = cordeanu_civil_war
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Iron Guard Brigade"
					}
					news_event = { id = r56.news_event.24 days = 2 random_days = 2 }
				}
				#Cordeanu's revolt, monarchist victory
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_government = neutrality
							has_government = democratic
						}
						has_global_flag = cordeanu_civil_war
					}
					clr_global_flag = cordeanu_civil_war
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Sentinel of the Motherland"
					}
					news_event = { id = r56.news_event.25 days = 2 random_days = 2 }
				}
			}
			#YUG DOD specific as the BFTB rework of YUG was a bit unsatisfactory
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = ROM
						original_tag = HUN
						original_tag = ALB
						original_tag = GRE
						original_tag = BUL
					}

					has_government = communism
					YUG = {
						has_completed_focus = YUG_pan_slavic_workers_congress
						has_government = communism
						has_country_flag = instigating_a_coup
					}
				}
				YUG = {
					add_to_faction = ROOT
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = YUG modifier = huge_increase }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { original_tag = USA }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = USA_REBEL
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
			#End of Turkish Civil War
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						original_tag = TUR
						OR = {
							has_government = communism
							has_government = neutrality
						}
					}
					original_tag = TUR
					has_global_flag = TUR_civil_war
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = TUR_civil_war_end
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = turkey.13 days = 1 }
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { original_tag = POR }
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = POR }
					remove_ideas = POR_civil_war_surrender_debuff
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { original_tag = SPR }
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = SPR }
					remove_ideas = SPR_r56_non_intervention_agreement
					set_capital = { state = 41 }
				}
			}

			# Greek CW
			if = { #MOD. Compressed.
				limit = {
					FROM = { original_tag = GRE }
					ROOT = { original_tag = GRE }

				set_capital = { state = 47 }

			#End of SCW

					}
				}

			#Romanian Civil War
			if = {

					FROM = {

					}
				}
				set_capital = { state = 46 }
			}

			#spread revolution siam commies win

					FROM = { original_tag = SIA }

###---> On Declare War <><> <><> <><>
	on_declare_war = {
		effect = {
			if = {	# Little Entente - Hungary war against
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							original_tag = HUN
							AND = {
								original_tag = AUS
								OR = {
									is_ally_with = HUN
									owns_state = 43 #budapest
								
								}
							}
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						has_idea = r56_YUG_little_entente
						OR = {
							original_tag = CZE
							original_tag = ROM
							original_tag = YUG
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = r56_HUN_if_we_go_to_war
					save_event_target_as = little_entente_attacker
					
				}
				log = "ROOT [ROOT.GetNameDef]"
				log = "FROM [FROM.GetNameDef]"
				FROM = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction = no
						}
						create_faction = "Little Entente"
					}
					
					every_other_country = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = r56_YUG_little_entente
							OR = {
								original_tag = CZE
								original_tag = ROM
								original_tag = YUG
							}
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = PREV
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = yugoslavia.25 hours = 12 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {	# Balkan Pact - Bulgaria war against
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						tag = BUL
					}
					FROM = {
						has_idea = r56_ROM_balkan_pact
						OR = {
							original_tag = GRE
							original_tag = ROM
							original_tag = TUR
							original_tag = YUG
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = r56_BUL_if_we_go_to_war
				}
				FROM = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction = no
						}
						create_faction = "Balkan Pact"
					}
					every_other_country = {
						limit = {
							has_idea = r56_ROM_balkan_pact
							OR = {
								original_tag = GRE
								original_tag = ROM
								original_tag = TUR
								original_tag = YUG
							}
							NOT = {
								has_war_with = PREV
							}
						}
						country_event = { id = yugoslavia.27 hours = 12 }
					}
				}
			}			
			if = { # BELGIAN event to arrest fascists after the invasion
				limit = {
					tag = GER
					has_government = fascism
					FROM = {
						tag = BEL
						has_government = democratic
						fascism < 0.5
					}
				}
				FROM = {
	                country_event = { id = belgium.131 hours = 18 random_hours = 5 }
				}
			}
			if = {# NEWS EVENT - Norwegian Neutrality violated by Germany, initial event #
				limit = {
					original_tag = NOR
					is_subject = no
					has_completed_focus = NOR_armed_neutrality_once_more
					has_defensive_war_with = GER

					has_idea = PRC_anti_jap_sentiment
					NOT = {
						has_idea = PRC_revanchism
					}
					FROM = { tag = JAP }
				}
				add_ideas = PRC_revanchism
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = PRC_restart_chinese_civil_war
					}
					OR = {
						AND = { tag = PRC FROM = { tag = CHI } }
						AND = { tag = CHI FROM = { tag = PRC } }
					}
				}
				PRC = {
					country_event = { id = china.108 }
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_completed_focus = PRC_found_our_nation
							}
						}
						drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
						set_cosmetic_tag = GCDcivilwar
						set_global_flag = PRC_civil_war_started
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								original_tag = ROOT
								original_tag = CHI
							}
						}
						add_timed_idea = {
							days = 570
							idea = PRC_until_the_bitter_end
						}
					}
					hidden_effect = {			#dongbei partisans
						country_event = { id = prc.49 days = 30 random_days = 10 }
					}
				}
			}
			# Middle Eastern countries get an option to join war against Israel
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = anti_israeli_coalition
					tag = EGY
					FROM = { tag = ISR }
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						capital_scope = {
							is_on_continent = middle_east
						}
						is_subject = no
						NOT = {
							original_tag = TUR
							original_tag = EGY
							original_tag = ISR
							has_war_with = EGY
							is_in_faction_with = ISR
							has_non_aggression_pact_with = ISR
						}
					}
					country_event = { id = egypt.49 days = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

###---> On New Term Election <><> <><> <><>
	on_new_term_election = {
		random_events = {		#costa rica elections of 1936
			100 = costa_rica.1
		}
		random_events = {
			100 = panama.1		#panama elections of 1936
		}
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = CHI
					has_government = neutrality
					NOT = { has_country_flag = KMT_party_chosen }
				}
				country_event = { id = kmt.279 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = MEX
					has_country_flag = election_1940
				}
				MEX = {
					country_event = { id = mexico_1940.4 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = AST }
				country_event = { id = r56_australia.8 }
				country_event = { id = r56_australia.9 }
				country_event = { id = r56_australia.10 }
				country_event = { id = r56_australia.11 }
				country_event = { id = r56_australia.12 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = FRA
					is_subject = no
					has_completed_focus = FRA_status_quo
					OR = {	#dont mention popular front if you arent/werent democratic
						has_government = communism
						has_government = democratic
					}
					communism > 0.5
					communism < 0.7	#I guess let them take full control
					#ensure France is definitely being sent the event
					exists = yes
					has_capitulated = no
					any_owned_state = {
						is_on_continent = europe
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						exists = yes
						has_capitulated = no
						OR = {
							is_subject_of = FRA
							any_owned_state = {
								is_on_continent = europe
							}
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						id = france.35
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = GER
					has_government = democratic
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_completed_focus = GER_restore_weimar
						}
						has_completed_focus = GER_establish_bundesrepublik
					}
				}
				country_event = r56.ger.60
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ENG
					has_government = democratic
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with_major = yes
					}
					country_event = r56_eng.8
				}
				else = {
					country_event = r56_eng.7
				}
			}
		}
	}

###---> On Puppet <><> <><> <><>
	on_puppet = {
		effect = {
			if = {	#Add victory points to Tonga
				limit = {
					tag = TON
				}
				add_victory_points = {
					province = 13419
					value = 2
				}
				add_victory_points = {
					province = 13420
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { tag = USA }
					USA = { has_government = communism }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { original_tag = AFG }
					}
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Mawlana Ryder Khadim"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/AFG/r56_portrait_AFG_Mawlana_Ryder_Khadim.dds"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = marxism
						traits = {
							revolutionary_poet
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { original_tag = AFG }
				}
				set_global_flag = achievement_AFG_has_been_puppeted
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = DEN
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_completed_focus = DEN_An_Appeal_to_the_Proletariat
						}
						has_government = communism
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_completed_focus = DEN_Galvanise_the_German_Minority
						}
						has_government = fascism
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_completed_focus = DEN_Initiate_Economic_Reforms
								has_completed_focus = DEN_Strengthen_the_Labour_Unions
							}
						}
						has_government = democratic
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_completed_focus = DEN_King_Christian_Coup
						}
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
				#Continue on
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = DEN
				}
				den_become_generic = yes
			}
			# The Father shall free Denmark
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = DEN
					FROM = {
						original_tag = SOV
					}
					SOV = { 
						has_government = neutrality
						has_completed_focus = SOV_the_third_rome
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = DEN_RUS
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Tsarin Olga Alexandrovna"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/LUX/r56_portrait_LUX_Duchess_Charlotte.dds"	#literally no female generic
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = absolute_monarchism
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = RAJ
					FROM = {
						NOT = {
							original_tag = ENG
						}
					}
				}
				load_focus_tree = r56_india_generic
				remove_ideas = {			
					RAJ_agrarian_Economy
					RAJ_agrarian_economy_famine 
					RAJ_agrarian_economy_recovery 
					RAJ_agrarian_economy_1 
					RAJ_agrarian_economy_2 
				}
				clr_country_flag = election_enabled
				clr_country_flag = raj_election_over
				clr_country_flag = army_research_decision
				clr_country_flag = RAJ_rail_act_support
				clr_country_flag = RAJ_agri_act_support
				clr_country_flag = RAJ_war_act_support
				clr_country_flag = ilp_conference_concluded
				clr_country_flag = independence_granted 
				clr_country_flag = ilp_south_asian_liberation
				clr_country_flag = integration_of_india
				clr_country_flag = ILP_victory 
				clr_country_flag = UP_victory
				clr_country_flag = INC_victory
				remove_ideas_with_trait = militiant_independence_activist
				set_country_flag = RAJ_famine_manual_trigger 	#Prevents Famine, which is hard to deal with without the focus tree
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					name = "AIFB"
					long_name = "All India Forward Bloc"
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Subhas Chandra Bose"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/RAJ/r56_portrait_RAJ_Subhas_Chadra_Bose.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = despotism
					traits = {
						indomitable_perseverance
					}
				}
			}

			if = {			#add this to prevent released countries from disobeying game rules		-	check for other game rules too! - Fantom
				limit = {	#added for BBA peace deals
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = ideology_join_faction
						option = EVENTS_ONLY
					}
				}
				set_rule = {
					can_join_factions = no
				}
			}

			## Add flag so USA can warn Germany if it rushes puppet/annex the netherlands/indonesia
			if = { #MOD. Compressed
				limit = {
					is_puppet_of = GER
					GER = {
						NOT = { has_government = democratic }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { tag = HOL }
					USA = {
						set_country_flag = { flag = USA_dutch_window days = 60 value = 1 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { tag = ENG }
					USA = {
						set_country_flag = { flag = USA_british_window days = 60 value = 1 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { tag = INS }
					USA = {
						set_country_flag = { flag = USA_dutch_window days = 60 value = 1 }
					}
				}
			}

			## Remove political advisors
			if = { #MOD. Optimized one step.
				limit = { has_government = communism }
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = democratic_reformer }
					remove_ideas_with_trait = democratic_reformer
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = staunch_monarchist }
					remove_ideas_with_trait = staunch_monarchist
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea_with_trait = fascist_demagogue }
					remove_ideas_with_trait = fascist_demagogue
				}
			}
			else_if = {

						option = RESISTANCE_25_MORE
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					add_ideas = idea_game_rule_resistance_increase_25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = resistance_rule
						option = RESISTANCE_25_LESS
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					add_ideas = idea_game_rule_resistance_decrease_25
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = special_forces_limit
						option = SPECIAL_FORCES_CAP_100
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					add_ideas = idea_game_rule_special_forces_cap_100
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { original_tag = EGY }
					EGY = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = EGY_BRITISH_PUPPET
					}
				}
				EGY = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = EGY
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						TAG = MPL
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							NOT= {
								has_cosmetic_tag = MPL_free
							}
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = MPL_free
				}
				unlock_national_focus = MPL_a_forgone_conclusion
			}
		}
	}

									rule = MPL_AI_BEHAVIOR
									option = DEFAULT
								}
							}
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = MPL_AI_BEHAVIOR
								option = MPL_MANDATE_STAY
							}
						}
					}
					set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 1 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = MPL_AI_BEHAVIOR
							option = MPL_MANDATE_COLLAPSE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 53 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = MPL_AI_BEHAVIOR
							option = MPL_PREPERATIONS_COLLAPSE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 80 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = MPL_AI_BEHAVIOR
							option = MPL_UNION_COLLAPSE
						}
					}
					set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 95 }
				}

				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = MPL_AI_BEHAVIOR
								option = MPL_UNION_COM
							}
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = MPL_AI_BEHAVIOR
								option = MPL_UNION_DEM
							}
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = MPL_AI_BEHAVIOR
								option = MPL_DISSOVLED
							}
						}
					}
					set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 60 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_historical_focus_on = no
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = MPL_AI_BEHAVIOR
								option = RANDOM
							}
						}
						EGY = {
							is_ai = yes
						}
					}
					random_list = { #remains of an old system i cba to change, sorry its done this way
						30 = { set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 1 } }
						20 = { set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 53 } }
						25 = { set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 80 } }
						15 = { set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 95 } }
						10 = { set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 60 } }
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_list = {  #MPL always collapse when EGY is a player to make game more interesting
						20 = { set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 53 } }
						25 = { set_variable = { MPL_path_selection = 80 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_unit_leader_level_up = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = promising
					skill > 2
				}
				remove_unit_leader_trait = promising
			}
		}
	}

	###---> On Subject Autonomy Level Change <><> <><> <><>
	on_subject_autonomy_level_change = {
		effect = {
			#Add to french tech group
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_autonomy_state = autonomy_colony
						has_autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
					}
					OVERLORD = { is_in_tech_sharing_group = french_research }
				}
				add_to_tech_sharing_group = french_research
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = VIN
					tag = CAM
					tag = LAO
					tag = FRI
					tag = MOR
					tag = TUN
					tag = SYR
					tag = LEB
					NOT = {
					    has_autonomy_state = autonomy_colony
						has_autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
					}
				}

				remove_from_tech_sharing_group = french_research
			}
		}
	}

	###---> On Dismantle Faction <><> <><> <><>
	#on_dismantle_faction = {
	#}
	
	on_leave_faction = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = RAJ
				}
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = RAJ
					NOT = { is_subject_of = ENG }
					has_cosmetic_tag = RAJ_UK
				}
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				retire_character = RAJ_lord_linlithgow
				retire_character = RAJ_lord_willingdon
				retire_character = RAJ_archibald_wavell
				retire_character = RAJ_louis_mountbatten
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					name = "UP"
					long_name = "Unionist Party"
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ROM
					has_country_flag = ROM_bound_to_comintern_flag
				}
				clr_country_flag = ROM_bound_to_comintern_flag
			}
		}
	}

	###---> On Uncapitulation <><> <><> <><>
	on_uncapitulation = {
		effect = {
			if = { #MOD. OPT
				limit = { original_tag = POL }
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				POL = { set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = POL_fascism_party_long name = POL_fascism_party } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = POL_The_Endecja_Movement
					}
					set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = POL_ND_party_long name = POL_ND_party }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = POL_The_Polish_Socialist_Party
					}
					set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = POL_PPS_party_long name = POL_PPS_party }
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_puppet_of = SOV }
							NOT = { has_government = communism }
						}
						set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = POL_democratic_party_long name = POL_democratic_party }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							is_puppet_of = SOV
							has_government = communism
						}
						POL = { set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = POL_PSL_long name = POL_PSL_party } }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = RUT
					RUT = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = RUT3
					}
				}
				RUT = {
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ENG
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Fallen Government"
					}
				}
				promote_character = ENG_clement_attlee
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = democratic
					long_name = "Labour Party"
					name = "Labour"
				}
			}
		}
	}

	###---> On Liberate (ONLY during peace conference) <><> <><> <><>
	on_liberate = {
		effect = {
			if = {	#Add victory points to Tonga
				limit = {
					tag = TON
				}
				add_victory_points = {
					province = 13419
					value = 2
				}
				add_victory_points = {
					province = 13420
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TAG = ZIM }
				ZIM = {
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes #British colony flag
				}
			}
			if = {			#French Lebanon gets a proper name
				limit = {
					tag = LEB
					has_cosmetic_tag = LEB_FRA
				}
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}

			if = { #MOD. OPT
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = starting_agencies
						option = ALL_COUNTRIES
					}
				}
				create_intelligence_agency = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = starting_agencies
						option = ALL_MAJORS_AND_STRONG_MINORS
					}
					capital_scope = {
						OR = {
							is_on_continent = north_america
							is_on_continent = europe
						}
					}
				}
				create_intelligence_agency = yes
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ENG
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Fallen Government"
					}
				}
				promote_character = ENG_clement_attlee
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = democratic
					long_name = "Labour Party"
					name = "Labour"
				}
			}
		}
		
	}

	on_war = { #MOD. OPT
		effect = {
			if = {	#From generic USA events - Eartharts wants to enlist upon USA entering a war
				limit = {
					tag = USA
					NOT = { has_global_flag = earhart_disappeared }
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.1 days = 2 }	#devoted maybe?
			}
			if = {	#From Swiss r56 tree - remove Swiss banking if in an offensive war
				limit = {
					tag = SWI
					has_global_flag = SWI_R56_focus_tree
					has_idea = SWI_banking
					has_offensive_war = yes
				}
				country_event = { id = EYE_swiss.12 }	#was 30, but banks will notice it earlier
			}
			if = {	#From Swiss r56 tree - lower Swiss banking if in a defensive war
				limit = {
					tag = SWI
					has_global_flag = SWI_R56_focus_tree
					has_idea = SWI_banking
					has_offensive_war = no
				}
				country_event = { id = EYE_swiss.13 }
			}
			if = {	#It can be saved here, so why not use it that way? - Fantom
				limit = {
					original_tag = ENG
					has_completed_focus = shadow_scheme_focus
				}
				country_event = { id = britain.24 days = 4 }
			}
			if = {	#From Belgian tree - replacing an old event with on_action - Fantom
				limit = {
					tag = BEL
					has_government = democratic
					NOT = {has_idea = BEL_national_union}
				}
				country_event = { id = belgium.27 hours = 12 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = GER
					ROOT = {
						NOT = {
							original_tag = GER
							original_tag = PRE
							original_tag = WUR
							original_tag = BAY
							original_tag = BAD
							original_tag = HAN
							original_tag = WGR
							original_tag = DDR
							original_tag = SHL
							original_tag = HES
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						limit = {
							has_unit_leader_flag = GER_military_mission_commander
						}
						set_nationality = GER
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = ITA
					ROOT = {
						NOT = {
							original_tag = ITA
							original_tag = NAP
							original_tag = VNZ
							original_tag = SAD
							original_tag = SIC
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						limit = {
							has_unit_leader_flag = ITA_military_mission_commander
						}
						set_nationality = ITA
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = POL_gamelin_convention
					tag = POL
					has_defensive_war = yes
					OR = {
						has_government = neutrality
						has_government = democratic
					}
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				if = {
					limit = { FRA = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
					FRA = { country_event = poland.126 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ENG = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
							is_in_faction_with = FRA
						}
					}
					ENG = { country_event = poland.126 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#Taken from vanilla, shall work for getting peace
	on_peace = {
		effect = {
			#Applies in case when AI was annexed mid-game without peace conference and thus kept some laws - preventing stucking in that law and making someone OP
			#add "generic" conscription laws since no longer capitulated - Fantom
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					has_war_support < 0.3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					add_idea = limited_conscription
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					has_war_support > 0.3
					has_war_support < 0.6
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					add_idea = extensive_conscription
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					has_war_support > 0.6
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					add_idea = service_by_requirement
				}
			}

			#add "generic" trade laws since no longer capitulated
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = full_host_reliance_r56_law
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = full_host_reliance_r56_law
					add_idea = limited_exports
				}
			}

			#add "generic" economy laws since no longer capitulated
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = evacuated_assets_r56_law
					has_war_support < 0.5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = evacuated_assets_r56_law
					add_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = evacuated_assets_r56_law
					has_war_support > 0.5
				}
				swap_ideas = {

	#ROOT - country that just went to peace
	on_peaceconference_ended = {
		effect = {
			#add "generic" conscription laws since no longer capitulated - Fantom
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					has_war_support < 0.3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					add_idea = limited_conscription
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					has_war_support > 0.3
					has_war_support < 0.6
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					add_idea = extensive_conscription
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					has_war_support > 0.6
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = influx_of_exiles_r56_law
					add_idea = service_by_requirement
				}
			}

			#add "generic" trade laws since no longer capitulated
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = full_host_reliance_r56_law
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = full_host_reliance_r56_law
					add_idea = limited_exports
				}
			}

			#add "generic" economy laws since no longer capitulated
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = evacuated_assets_r56_law
					has_war_support < 0.5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = evacuated_assets_r56_law
					add_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = evacuated_assets_r56_law
					has_war_support > 0.5
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = evacuated_assets_r56_law
					add_idea = war_economy
				}
			}

			#try to fix war propaganda decision bug, open the way to mini exploits but would be exploited by increased national morale.
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = war_propaganda_campaign_running
				}
				clr_country_flag = war_propaganda_campaign_running
			}
			#wait we are not that big? Return to generic Hungary
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = HUN
					has_cosmetic_tag = HUN_EMPIRE
					AUS = {
						exists = yes
					}
					num_of_controlled_states < 7
				}
				drop_cosmetic_tag  = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = r56_yalta_script_is_a_go
					ROOT = {
						TAG = SOV
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						WGR = {
							is_ai = no
						}
					}
					WGR = { change_tag_from = GER }
				}
				SOV = {
					country_event = { id = r56.ger.3 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = r56_yalta_script_is_a_go
					OR = {
						country_exists = DDR
						country_exists = WGR
					}
				}
				country_event = r56.ger.5	#second yalta fixing event
			}		
		}
	}

	on_unit_leader_created = {

								has_trait = inshore_fighter

			}

				limit = {

	on_send_volunteers = { # called when a country send volunteers to another # ROOT is sender, FROM is receiver
		effect = {
			if = { #Bulgaria has sent volunteers to Spanish Republicans/Nationalists (LaR)
				limit = {
					tag = ROM
					FROM = { original_tag = SPR }
					has_dlc = "La Resistance"
					SPR_scw_in_progress = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = { tag = SPD }
					}
					set_country_flag = ROM_sent_volunteers_to_SPD_flag
				}
				else = {
					set_country_flag = ROM_sent_volunteers_to_SPA_flag
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = BUL
					FROM = { original_tag = SPR }
					NOT = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" }
					FROM = { has_civil_war = yes }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							OR = {
								has_government = democratic
								has_government = communism
							}
						}
					}
					set_country_flag = ROM_sent_volunteers_to_SPD_flag
				}
				else = {
					set_country_flag = ROM_sent_volunteers_to_SPA_flag
				}
			}

			if = { #"solving bug" which prevented pro-Republican volunteers to get proper supply - remove this if bug was resolved in any other way - Fantom
				limit = {	# the issue is probably in setting capital for SCW rebels
					SPR_scw_in_progress = yes
					FROM = {
						original_tag = SPR
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					give_military_access = ROOT
				}
			}

			if = {		#slight influence buffs for sending volunteers to specific nations	-Fantom
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								has_idea = r56_generic_international_brigades_idea
							}
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						add_timed_idea = { idea = r56_generic_international_brigades_idea days = 60 }
					}
				}
				else = {		#just a little buff to prevent stacking
					FROM = {
						modify_timed_idea = {
							idea = r56_generic_international_brigades_idea
							days = 20
						}
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								has_idea = r56_generic_civic_defense_force_idea
							}
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						add_timed_idea = { idea = r56_generic_civic_defense_force_idea days = 60 }
					}
				}
				else = {		#just a little buff to prevent stacking
					FROM = {
						modify_timed_idea = {
							idea = r56_generic_civic_defense_force_idea
							days = 20
						}
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								has_idea = r56_generic_foreign_freedom_fighters_idea
							}
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						add_timed_idea = { idea = r56_generic_foreign_freedom_fighters_idea days = 60 }
					}
				}
				else = {		#just a little buff to prevent stacking
					FROM = {
						modify_timed_idea = {
							idea = r56_generic_foreign_freedom_fighters_idea
							days = 20
						}
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								has_idea = r56_generic_broad_paramilitary_squadrons_idea
							}
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						add_timed_idea = { idea = r56_generic_broad_paramilitary_squadrons_idea days = 60 }
					}
				}
				else = {		#just a little buff to prevent stacking
					FROM = {
						modify_timed_idea = {
							idea = r56_generic_broad_paramilitary_squadrons_idea
							days = 20
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

	#FROM is country getting invited.
	on_offer_join_faction = {
		effect = {
			#Remove anti_soviet_pact if joining commie Soviet in faction
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							original_tag = FRA
							FROM = { original_tag = USA }
						}
						AND = {
							original_tag = USA
							FROM = { original_tag = FRA }
						}
					}
					FRA = { has_government = fascism }
					USA = { has_government = fascism }
				}
				news_event = { id = r56.news_event.21 hours = 12 }
			}
		}
	}

	on_join_faction = {
		effect = {
			#Franco American Fascist alliance
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							original_tag = FRA
							FROM = { original_tag = USA }
						}
						AND = {
							original_tag = USA
							FROM = { original_tag = FRA }
						}
					}
				}
				news_event = { id = r56.news_event.21 hours = 12 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = RAJ
				}
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = DEN
				}
				set_country_flag = den_has_joined_faction
			}
			
		}
	}

    on_daily_RAJ = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = raj_election_over
					NOT = { has_country_flag = independence_granted }
					tag = RAJ
					exists = yes
					is_subject = yes
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					pak_influence = pak_influence_daily
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					ind_influence = ind_influence_daily
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							pak_influence_daily < 0
						}
						check_variable = {
							pak_influence < 1
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						pak_influence_daily = 0
					}
					set_variable = {
						pak_influence = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_weekly_IRQ = {	#was daily, changed to weekly, doesn't have to be checked thaaaat often
		effect = {
			if = {	### British peace offer
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = IRQ_historical_golden_square_coup
					surrender_progress > 0.5
					ENG = {						#sanity check to see if UK is powerful
						is_subject = no
						is_faction_leader = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					any_owned_state = {			#a check to see if UK is the one who is doing the pushing
						is_controlled_by = ENG
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = iraq_hist.5 }
			}
		}
	}

	on_monthly_MPL = {
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_power_balance = {
						id = MPL_power_balance
					}
				}
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = MPL_city_random
					min = 1
					max = 7
					integer = yes
				}
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = MPL_jew_militia
					min = 1
					max = 3
					integer = yes
				}
				set_variable_to_random = {
					var = MPL_arab_militia
					min = 1
					max = 5
					integer = yes
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = MPL_no_raid_chance
						}
						#DO NOTHING
					}
					1 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = MPL_raid_chance
						}
						#TRIGGER EVENT
						random_list = {
							30 = {
								country_event = { #Irgun wins clash
									id = mandate_palestine.301
									days = 1
									random_days = 25
									random_hours = 24

		effect = {
			#
			# (E-L)/4 ~ diff/month
			# (50-75)/4 = -6.25 ~ -6
			# (50-20)/4 = 7.5 ~ 8
			#
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = DEN
					den_stratas_enabled = yes
				}
				den_calculate_eqilibirum_monthly = yes
			}
		}
	}
